SELECT m0.nombre, m0.id, s."Id", s."CentroPoblado", s."Tipo", s.id0
FROM (
    SELECT m.nombre, m.id
    FROM municipio AS m
    WHERE m.id = @__id_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS m0
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT c.id AS "Id", c.nombre AS "CentroPoblado", t.nombre AS "Tipo", t.id AS id0, c.municipio_id
    FROM centros_poblados AS c
    INNER JOIN tipo_centro_poblado AS t ON c.tipo = t.id
) AS s ON m0.id = s.municipio_id
ORDER BY m0.id, s."Id"

FROM (
    SELECT m.nombre, m.id
    FROM municipio AS m
    WHERE m.id = @__id_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS m0
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT c.id AS "Id", c.nombre AS "CentroPoblado", t.nombre AS "Tipo", t.id AS id0, c.municipio_id
    FROM centros_poblados AS c

SELECT m0.nombre, m0.id, s."Id", s."CentroPoblado", s."Tipo", s.id0
FROM (
    SELECT m.nombre, m.id
    FROM municipio AS m
    WHERE m.id = @__id_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS m0
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT c.id AS "Id", c.nombre AS "CentroPoblado", t.nombre AS "Tipo", t.id AS id0, c.municipio_id
    FROM centros_poblados AS c
    INNER JOIN tipo_centro_poblado AS t ON c.tipo = t.id
) AS s ON m0.id = s.municipio_id
ORDER BY m0.id, s."Id"

SELECT m0.nombre, m0.id, s."Id", s."CentroPoblado", s."Tipo", s.id0
FROM (
    SELECT m.nombre, m.id
    FROM municipio AS m
    WHERE m.id = @__id_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS m0
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT c.id AS "Id", c.nombre AS "CentroPoblado", t.nombre AS "Tipo", t.id AS id0, c.municipio_id
    FROM centros_poblados AS c
    INNER JOIN tipo_centro_poblado AS t ON c.tipo = t.id
) AS s ON m0.id = s.municipio_id
ORDER BY m0.id, s."Id"

    FROM municipio AS m
    WHERE m.id = @__id_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS m0

    SELECT c.id AS "Id", c.nombre AS "CentroPoblado", t.nombre AS "Tipo", t.id AS id0, c.municipio_id

    FROM municipio AS m
    WHERE m.id = @__id_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS m0
